### Post by Vasto on 2008-05-30
Ubuntu 8.04 LTS 64bit

I tried to compile the newest bitpim from source because the one in the repository is pretty out dated.
I followed the directions from [BitPim](http://www.bitpim.org/developer.html)
> apt-get install alien
apt-get install libgtk2.0-dev freeglut3-dev python2.5-dev
wget [http://easynews.dl.sourceforge.net/wxpython/wxPython2.8-2.8.7.1-1.src.rpm](http://easynews.dl.sourceforge.net/wxpython/wxPython2.8-2.8.7.1-1.src.rpm)
rpmbuild --rebuild --define 'pyver 2.5' wxPython2.8-2.8.7.1-1.src.rpm

It kept aborting so I outputted the terminal to a text file (although when I compare the last line in the terminal to the last line in the text file, they don't match.)

Here is my output

### Post by Thelasko on 2008-06-02
I don't have any advice for you.  I just thought I would wish you good luck.  The Bitpim package has become horribly out of date and there doesn't seem to be any effort into getting a back port of the latest version.

I noticed Intrepid Ibex will have the latest and greatest version, but the package also requires the latest version of python.  That may be your problem.

There is a Debian package on the Bitpim page, the architecture is i386.  I wonder if that could be forced to work on x64?

---

### Post by Thelasko on 2008-06-04
I have found Wammu (not the bank) works well for syncing all of my phones (even ones it says it doesn't officially support) and moto4lin works fairly well for file transfers etc. Although, it has to be run as root(sudo), which I don't like.

---
